    if (window.pageYOffset >= wallpaperPosition.top && !isAdded) {\n                wallpaper.classList.add('am-is-sticky');\n                wallpaper.parentNode.insertBefore(placeholder, wallpaper);\n                isAdded = true;\n            } else if (window.pageYOffset < wallpaperPosition.top && isAdded) {\n                wallpaper.classList.remove('am-is-sticky');\n                wallpaper.parentNode.removeChild(placeholder);\n                isAdded = false;\n            }\n        });\n    </script>\n        <div class=\"am-page-ad\">\n            <div
